 agar aapse koi kahe ki ek gaanv kii jansankhya beete 97 saal se sthir he to aapako yah baat paheli lagegi, magar he hakeekat
 Dhanora in Betul district of Madhya Pradesh is a village where the population was 1700 in the year 1922 and it remains the same today
 yahaan kisi bhi parivaar main do se zyada bachche nahin hai
 This is due to the absence of discrimination between sons and daughters
 duniya main samasyaon kaa bada kaaran jansankhya ko mana jaataa he, kyonki har desh-pradesh or gaanv kii jansankhya main lagaataar ijapha ho rahaa he
 At the same time facilities or simply say that the resource is limited
 baitool kaa dhanora gaanv in sthitiyon main duniya ke liye parivaar niyojan ke kshetra main brands ambesder he, kyonki yahaan jansankhya bad nahin rahi he
 Dhanora is the village where the population has remained stable for the last 97 years
 yani in saalon main gaanv kii jansankhya 1,700 se aage nahin badi
 how did this happen? It also has an interesting story
 es
 K
 mahobia bataate he ki san 1922 main yahaan congress kaa ek sammelan hua tha jisamen shaamil hone kasturba gandhi ai thim
 He gave the slogan of 'small family, happy family' to the villagers for a happy life
 kasturba gandhi kii baat ko graminon ne pathar kii lakeer mana or phir gaanv main parivaar niyojan kaa silsilaa shuru ho gaya
 The elders say that the message of Kasturba Gandhi sat on the hearts and minds of the people here that after 1922, there was tremendous awareness among the villagers for family planning in the village
 lagbhag har parivaar ne ek yaa do bacchon par parivaar niyojan karavaaya, jisase dhire-dhire gaanv kii jansankhya sthir hone lagi
 The people here have also abolished the practice of growing a family in the desire of sons and they consider family planning to be necessary after the birth of one or two daughters
 parivaar niyojan ke maamle main yah gaanv ek model ban gaya he
 Be it daughter or son, after two children adopting family planning, the sex ratio here is much better than elsewhere
 itnaa hi nahin, beti-bete main fark jaisi maansikta yahaan dekhne ko nahin milti
 Villagers say that there are many villages around Dhanora, whose population has increased four to five times compared to what it was 50 years ago, but the population of Dhanora village still remains 1,700
 gaanv ke swasthya kaaryakarta jagadish singh parihaar bataate hai ki unhen kabhi graminon ko parivaar niyojan karne ke liye baadhya nahin karnaa padaa
 The result of awareness among the local people is that they get family planning after two children
